# Awesome Rust [![build badge ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-unofficial/awesome-rust) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rust-unofficial/awesome-rust)](https://github.com/rust-unofficial/awesome-rust/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg?branch=main)](https://github.com/rust-unofficial/awesome-rust/actions/workflows/rust.yml) [![Track Awesome List](https://www.trackawesomelist.com/badge.svg)](https://www.trackawesomelist.com/rust-unofficial/awesome-rust/)

A curated list of Rust code and resources.

If you want to contribute, please read [this](CONTRIBUTING.md).

### Build system

* [Cargo](https://crates.io/) â€” the Rust package manager
  * [cargo-all-features ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features) - A configurable subcommand to simplify testing, building and much more for all combinations of features [![CI ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/frewsxcv/cargo-all-features/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
  * [cargo-benchcmp](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-benchcmp) â€” A utility to compare Rust micro-benchmarks
  * [cargo-bitbake](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-bitbake) â€” A cargo extension that can generate BitBake recipes utilizing the classes from meta-rust
  * [cargo-cache](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-cache) â€” inspect/manage/clean your cargo cache (`~/.cargo/`/`${CARGO_HOME}`), print sizes etc [![Build Status ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache)](https://github.com/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/workflows/ci/badge.svg?branch=master)](https://github.com/matthiaskrgr/cargo-cache/actions)
  * [cargo-check](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-check) â€” A wrapper around `cargo rustc -- -Zno-trans` which can be helpful for running a faster compile if you only need correctness checks
  * [cargo-commander](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-commander) â€” A subcommand for `cargo` to run CLI commands similar to how the scripts section in `package.json` works [![Build and test ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simonhyll/cargo-commander) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/simonhyll/cargo-commander)](https://github.com/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/simonhyll/cargo-commander/actions/workflows/build.yml)
  * [cargo-count](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-count) â€” lists source code counts and details about cargo projects, including unsafe statistics
  * [cargo-deb](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-deb) â€” Generates binary Debian packages
  * [cargo-deps](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-deps) â€” build dependency graphs of Rust projects
  * [cargo-do](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-do) â€” run multiple cargo commands in a row
  * [cargo-ebuild](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-ebuild) â€” cargo extension that can generate ebuilds using the in-tree eclasses
  * [cargo-edit](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-edit) â€” allows you to add and list dependencies by reading/writing to your Cargo.toml file from the command line
  * [cargo-generate ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cargo-generate/cargo-generate) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/cargo-generate/cargo-generate)](https://github.com/cargo-generate/cargo-generate) A generator of a rust project by leveraging a pre-existing git repository as a template.
  * [cargo-graph](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-graph) â€” updated fork of `cargo-dot` with additional features. Unmaintained, see `cargo-deps`
  * [cargo-info](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-info) â€” queries crates.io for crates details from command line
  * [cargo-license](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-license) â€” A cargo subcommand to quickly view the licenses of all dependencies.
  * [cargo-limit](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-limit) â€” Cargo with less noise: warnings are skipped until errors are fixed, Neovim integration, etc. [![build badge ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alopatindev/cargo-limit) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/alopatindev/cargo-limit)](https://github.com/alopatindev/cargo-limit/actions/workflows/rust.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/alopatindev/cargo-limit/actions)
  * [cargo-make](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-make) â€” Rust task runner and build tool. [![build badge ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sagiegurari/cargo-make) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sagiegurari/cargo-make)](https://github.com/sagiegurari/cargo-make/workflows/CI/badge.svg?branch=master)](https://github.com/sagiegurari/cargo-make/actions)
  * [cargo-modules](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-modules) â€” A cargo plugin for showing a tree-like overview of a crate's modules.
  * [cargo-multi](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-multi) â€” runs specified cargo command on multiple crates
  * [cargo-outdated](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-outdated) â€” displays when newer versions of Rust dependencies are available, or out of date
  * [cargo-rdme ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orium/cargo-rdme) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/orium/cargo-rdme)](https://github.com/orium/cargo-rdme) [[cargo-rdme](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-rdme)] â€” Cargo subcommand to create your README from your crateâ€™s documentation.   * [cargo-release](https://crates.io/crates/cargo-release) â€” tool for releasing git-managed cargo project, build, tag, publish, doc and push [![Rust ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/crate-ci/cargo-release) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/crate-ci/cargo-release)](https://github.com/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/crate-ci/cargo-release/actions/workflows/rust.yml)

### Embedded

[Rust Embedded](https://rust-embedded.org/) focuses on improving the end-to-end experience of using Rust in resource-constrained environments and non-traditional platforms. See [awesome-embedded-rust ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust)](https://github.com/rust-embedded/awesome-embedded-rust) for a curated, and more extended list of embedded Rust resources.

* Arduino
  * [avr-rust/ruduino ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avr-rust/ruduino) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/avr-rust/ruduino)](https://github.com/avr-rust/ruduino) Reusable components for the Arduino Uno.
* Cross compiling
  * [japaric/rust-cross ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/japaric/rust-cross) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/japaric/rust-cross)](https://github.com/japaric/rust-cross) â€” everything you need to know about cross compiling Rust programs
  * [japaric/xargo ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/japaric/xargo) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/japaric/xargo)](https://github.com/japaric/xargo) â€” effortless cross compilation of Rust programs to custom bare-metal targets like ARM Cortex-M
* Espressif
  * [esp-rs](https://github.com/esp-rs) home to a number of community projects enabling the use of the Rust programming language on various SoCs and modules produced by Espressif Systems.
* Firmware
  * [oreboot/oreboot ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oreboot/oreboot) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/oreboot/oreboot)](https://github.com/oreboot/oreboot) â€” oreboot is a fork of coreboot, with C removed, written in Rust
* nRF
  * [nrf-rs/nrf-hal ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nrf-rs/nrf-hal) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nrf-rs/nrf-hal)](https://github.com/nrf-rs/nrf-hal) â€” A Rust HAL for the nRF family of devices

### FFI

See also [Foreign Function Interface](https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/first-edition/ffi.html), [The Rust FFI Omnibus](http://jakegoulding.com/rust-ffi-omnibus/) (a collection of examples of using code written in Rust from other languages) and [FFI examples written in Rust ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples)](https://github.com/alexcrichton/rust-ffi-examples).

## Registries

A registry allows you to publish your Rust libraries as crate packages, to share them with others publicly and privately.

* [Cloudsmith :heavy_dollar_sign:](https://cloudsmith.com/product/formats/cargo-registry) â€” A fully managed package management SaaS, with first-class support for public and private Cargo/Rust registries (plus many others). Has a generous free-tier and is also completely free for open-source.
* [Crates](https://crates.io) â€” The official public registry for Rust/Cargo.
* [w4/chartered ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/w4/chartered) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/w4/chartered)](https://github.com/w4/chartered) - A private, authenticated, permissioned Cargo registry [![CI ![GitHub Repo Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/w4/chartered) ![GitHub last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/w4/chartered)](https://github.com/w4/chartered/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/w4/chartered/actions/workflows/ci.yml)
